of Belfast will elect one of their number and the Head Constables of
theSixCountiesand the County Borough of Londonderry, willelect
oneoftheirnumber toacton theRepresentativeBody .
Sergeants. The Sergeantsof the County Borough of Belfastwill

Tyrone , and Londonderry and the County Borough of Londonderry,
willelectone of theirnumber , and the Sergeantsof the Countiesof
Antrim ,Down and Armagh willelectone oftheirnumber to acton the
RepresentativeBody .
Constables. The Constablesin the County Borough of Belfast
willelecttwo of theirnumber ,the Constablesof the Countiesof Fer-
managh and Tyrone willelectone of theirnumber ,the Constablesof
theCountiesofAntrim and Londonderryand theCounty Borough of
Londonderrywillelectone of theirnumber, and the Constablesof
Armagh and Down willelectone of theirnumber to act on the Repre-
sentativeBody .

election .

The votingpapershaving been duly counted willbe sealedup in

be destroyed.

inthepresenceofscrutineersappointedfrom the HeadquartersStation,
one foreach rank,and willdeclarewhich candidateiselected.

totheresultoftheelection,thenames ofthecandidatesand thenumber
of votes recorded for each shall be circulated to each station in the Area .

(m )-No person shallcontrol, direct, influence, or in any other

area,and vacanciesshallnot arisesave in the caseof a representative
leavingthe Force,changing rank,or resignationfrom the Representa-

goingrulesby members of the Force ofthe rank and in the areawhere
the vacancy occurred.
(7)-The RepresentativeBodies may make applicationto the
InspectorGeneralforany informationthey desireto obtainwith a view
to assist them in their deliberations .
(8)-Each RepresentativeBody shallchooseitsChairman and
Secretaryfrom among itsown members . Where thereisan equality
ofvotesregardingany pointwhichmay be underconsideration,the
Chairman shallhave a second or castingvote.
(9)-Leave (not to count againstannual leave)shallbe givenfor
attendanceat the Meetings of the RepresentativeBodies, and every
such attendanceshall,as regardsallowancesand expenses,be deemed
to be an occasionof Policeduty .
(10)-The electionsshalltake placeannuallyin the month of
September, the retiringmembers being eligiblefor re-election, and
annual Meetings of the Representative Bodies shallbe held in the
month ofOctober,on a date and at a placeto be fixedby the Inspector
General. Meetingsforspecialpurposesshallbe held as occasionarises
and on suchdatesand at suchplacesas the InspectorGeneralmay
determine. No meetings of the RepresentativeBodies are to extend
beyond threedays,save by the sanctionof the InspectorGeneral.
(11)-The two RepresentativeBodiesmay by agreementsit
togetheras a jointRepresentativeBody forany specialpurpose, or
regularlyforallpurposesof common interest. They may alsobe
summoned to sitas a jointRepresentativeBody by the Inspector
Generalfortheconsiderationofany questionreferredtothem by him.

ERN IRELAND ,
1923. No. 35 .
BY THE LORDS JUSTICES AND PRIVY COUNCIL IN NORTHERN IRELAND .
WILLIAM MOORE .
WHEREAS by the Representationof the People Order made
under section13 ofthe Representationofthe PeopleAct ,1918 (in thisOrder referredto as " theAct of1918 "),His Majestyhas been pleased
by Order in Council,amongst othermatters,to prescribethe forms to
be used for registrationpurposes so far as respectslocalgovernment
franchise :
AND WHEREAS by section40 (2)ofthe Act of 1918 any Order
in Council made thereunder may be revoked or varied as occasion
requiresby any subsequent Order in Council:
AND WHEREAS by the Local Government (Franchise) Act
(Northern Ireland),1923 (hereinafterreferredtoas " theAct of 1923 "),
theAct of 1918in itsapplicationto localgovernmentfranchisesin
Northern Ireland was amended :
AND WHEREAS by section1 (2)oftheAct of1923 itisenacted
that the Governor may by Order in the Privy Council of Northern
Ireland,prescribethe forms to be used forregistrationpurposesso far
as respectsthe localgovernment franchises,and may by any such order
(withtheapprovaloftheSecretaryofState)make suchalterationsof
the forms prescribedby or under section13 of the Representationof
thePeopleAct,1918,intheirapplicationtothesefranchisesinNorthern
Ireland,as appear to him to be necessaryor proper,forthe purposeof
givingeffectto the Act of 1923 :
AND WHEREAS alterationsof certainof the forms prescribed
by or under section13 of the Act of 1918 in theirapplicationto local
government franchisesin Northern Irelandare necessaryand proper
forthepurpose ofgivingeffectto the Act of 1923 ;
NOW WE the LORDS JUSTICES OF NORTHERN IRELAND
by and with the adviceand consentof His Majesty'sPrivy Councilin
Northern Irelandwith the approval of the Secretaryof Stateand by
virtueand inpursuanceofthe powers vestedin US forthatpurposeby
the Act of 1923 and of allotherpowers enablingUS do hereby order
as follows : -
Form (1) Man's Claim, and Form (2) Woman's Claim in
ScheduleIII.of the Representationof the People Order shallin
theirapplicationto local government franchisesin Northern
Ireland be alteredand the forms set out in the Schedule to this
Order shall be substituted for the said Forms .
GIVEN at Belfast,this29th day ofJune ,1923.
BY THEIR EXCELLENCIES ' COMMAND ,
R. Dawson Bates .

MADE BY THE MINISTRY OF FINANCE FOR NORTHERN IRELAND UNDER

& 13 GEO .5,С. 7).
1923. No. 47 .
WHEREAS itisprovidedby section12 (3)ofthe Unemployment
InsuranceAct, 1920 (hereinafterreferredto as " the 1920 Act "),as
the 1920 Act appliesto Northern Irelandand in particularas amended
initsapplicationto NorthernIrelandby section7 ofthe Unemployment
InsuranceAct (Northern Ireland),1922,thatsuch sum as the Ministry
of Finance forNorthern Irelandmay direct,not exceedingone-eighth
ofthe receiptspaidintothe Northern IrishUnemployment Fund after
certaindeductionsreferredto in the saidsectionhave been made ,shall
inaccordancewithRegulationsmade by thesaidMinistrybe applied
as an appropriationin aid of the moneys provided by Parliament for
the purposeof the salaries, remunerationand expensesmentioned
in the saidsection12 (3)of the 1920 Act .
NOW THEREFORE , the Ministry of Finance for Northern
Ireland,by virtueofthe powers hereinbeforementioned,hereby makes
the followingregulations:-
1. These Regulationsmay be citedas the Unemployment In-
surance(NorthernIreland)(AppropriationsinAid)Regulations,1923.
2.-(i) In theseRegulations, unlessthe contextotherwisere-
quires :-
"theMinistry" means theMinistryofLabour forNorthern
Ireland .
ود
"The Fund means theNorthern IrishUnemployment Fund
establishedunder Section14 (1)ofthe 1920 Act as modifiedand
adapted by the Government of Ireland(Adaptation of Unem-
ploymentInsuranceActs) Order, 1922,made under Section69
of the Government of IrelandAct ,1920.
(ii)The InterpretationAct (NorthernIreland),1921(12 Geo.5.
c.4)appliesforthepurposeoftheinterpretationoftheseRegulations
as itappliesforthe purpose of the interpretationof an Act of Parlia-
ment .
3. Whenever any payment ismade from theVoteforUnemploy-
ment InsurancetotheFund undertheUnemployment InsuranceActs
(NorthernIreland)1920to 1923,a correspondingpayment shall(save
as ishereinafterprovidedin Regulation8) be made simultaneously
fromtheFund and appliedasan appropriationinaidoftheMinistry's
Voteundersubsection(3)ofSectiontwelveofthe1920Act,asamended
by Sectionseven of the Unemployment InsuranceAct (Northern
Ireland), 1922.

Continuous Period of Unemployment (Transitional).
MADE BY THE MINISTRY OF LABOUR FOR NORTHERN IRELAND UNDER
THE UNEMPLOYMENT INSURANCE ACT (NORTHERN IRELAND ),1923 .
1923. No. 34 .
For thepurposeofprovidingforthetransitionfrom theprovisions
ofthe Unemployment InsuranceActs (Northern Ireland),1920 to 1922,
relatingto continuousperiodsof unemployment to the provisionsof
sectionsix of the Unemployment InsuranceAct (Northern Ireland),
1923 (hereinafterreferredto asthe Act of1923),the MinistryofLabour
forNorthern Irelandby virtueofthe powers conferredon itby the said
sectionand ofallotherpowers enablingitinthatbehalf,hereby makes
the followingregulations:-
1. Where a continuousperiodofunemployment of not lessthan
one week occurs before the commencement of section six of the Act of
1923and isfollowedby a continuousperiodofunemployment beginning
on a date between the commencement ofthatsectionand the thirdday
ofMay ,1923,thosetwo continuousperiodsof unemployment shall,if
separatedby a periodof not more than sixweeks be treatedas a con-
tinuousperiodof unemployment .

## Page 117

Courts of Referees(Amending ). 111
2.Any daysofunemploymentoccurringbetweenthecommence-
ment ofsectionsixofthe Act of 1923 and the thirdday of May ,1923,
which,togetherwith any days of unemployment occurringbeforethe
commencement of that section, might have been treatedunder the
Unemployment InsuranceActs (NorthernIreland),1920to 1922,as a
continuousperiod of unemployment , may , togetherwith such days,
be so treated,notwithstandingthe repealofthe provisionsof the last-
mentioned Acts relatingto the computation of continuousperiodsof
unemployment .
3. A continuousperiod of unemployment which begins before
and continues after the commencement of section six of the Act of
1923 shall,togetherwith :-
(a) any previouscontinuousperiodof unemployment of not less
than one week from which itisseparatedby an intervalof
not more than six weeks ; and
(b) any subsequentcontinuousperiodof unemployment from
which itisseparatedby a periodof lessthan threeweeks.
be treatedas a continuousperiodof unemployment .
4. In these Regulations, the expression"continuous period of
unemployment " where itrefersto a periodbeginningafterthe com-
mencement of sectionsixof the Act of 1923 has the same meaning as
inthatAct,and where itrefersto a periodoccurringorbeginningbefore
the commencement of that sectionhas the same meaning as in the
Unemployment InsuranceActs (Northern Ireland), 1920 to 1922.
5. These Regulationsmay be cited as the Unemployment In-
surance (Continuous Period of Unemployment ) (Transitional) Regu-
lations(Northern Ireland), 1923.
(L.S.)

Schedules .
THE INSURANCE INDUSTRY .
1.The InsuranceIndustryshallconsistof the undertakingsof
all persons or bodies of persons whether corporate or incorporate
and whether establishedwithinor without Northern Irelandengaged
inNorthern Irelandin allor any ofthe followingclassesofbusiness:-
(a) the grantingof insurancesunder contract.
(b) the administrationof any system of insuranceestablished
by Act of the Imperial Parliament or the Parliament of
Northern Ireland .
SCOPE OF SCHEME .
2.- (1) Subjectto the provisionsofthe Scheme allpersonsofthe
age of sixteenand upwards employed in NorthernIrelandin the
InsuranceIndustryunder any contractof serviceorapprenticeship
writtenor oralwhether expressedorimpliedand whether theemployed
personispaid by the employer or by some other personand whether
under one or more employers and whether paid by time or by thepiece
or partlyby time and partlyby the pieceor otherwiseor exceptinthe
caseofa contractofapprenticeshipwithoutany money payment shall
(unlesstheiremployment isincludedin the employments specifiedin
Part II of the FirstSchedule of the PrincipalAct as amended by any
subsequent enactment) be insuredagainstunemployment in manner
hereby provided .
(2) The scheme shallnot apply to any personswho come within
any of the following classes:-

## Page 127

InsuranceIndustrySpecialScheme (Amendment ). 121
(a) Personswho areordinarilyengagedwhetherundera single
employeror under two or more employerspartlyin the
InsuranceIndustryand partlyoutsidethatIndustryinsome
occupation employment in which makes them employed
personswithin the meaning of the Act as amended by any
subsequent enactment if such persons are ordinarilyand
mainly dependent fortheirlivelihoodon theirearningsin
the occupationoutsidethe InsuranceIndustry.
(6) Persons employed by or under the Crown or under any local
or other public authority .
(c) Persons in the employment of Insurance Committees estab-

B. DURATION OF BENEFIT .
1. Benefitshallbe paid at the standard ratesduring periodsof
unemployment which in the aggregatedo not exceed one-sixthof the
periodorthe aggregateofthe periodssubsequentto the 8th November ,
1920, during which the insured person has been employed in the
InsuranceIndustry provided that :-
(i) Such benefitshallnot be paid for more than twenty-six
weeks during any continuous period of unemployment or
any seriesof periodsof unemployment liableto aggregation.
(ii) Any seriesof periodsof unemployment in the intervalsof
which thereisno periodof continuousemployment in the
InsuranceIndustryof at leastthirteenweeks shallbe liable
to aggregation .
(iii) As from the commencement of any periodwhich ispreceded
by a periodof not lessthan twenty-sixweeks during which
the insured person has receivedno benefiteitherat the
standard rate or at the lesser rate hereinafter mentioned no
account shallbe taken in applying the two foregoingpro-
visionsto the case of such insuredperson of any benefitat
the standard ratereceivedby him priorto the date of such
commencement .
(iv) A periodof unemployment shallnot be deemed tocommence
untilthe insuredperson has made applicationfor benefit
in the prescribedmanner but the Board may where good
cause isshown allow some earlierdate to be substituted for
the date of application.
(v) Any periodsubsequentto the seventeenthday of October,

has been received under the provisionsof the Adapted

PART II .
(CONDITIONS FOR THE RECEIPT OF BENEFIT ).
An insuredpersonin orderto qualifyforreceiptof benefitunder
the Scheme must satisfythe followingconditions:-
(1) He must sincethe8thNovember,1920,have beenemployed
in the InsuranceIndustryin each of thirteenweeks .
(2) He must be (a) capableof and (6)availableforwork and (c)
genuinelyand constantlyseekingbut unableto obtainsuitableemploy-
ment . Provided thatwhere itisheld that an insuredpersondoes not
satisfythisconditionhisapplicationifrenewed shallbe reviewedfrom
time to time at the expirationof periodsof not lessthan sixweeks
(3) He must make applicationforbenefitintheprescribedmanner .
(4) He must not have exhausted his right to benefitunder the
Scheme .
(5) His unemployment must not be due to participationin a
tradedispute. Provided that itshallnot be necessaryto satisfythis
conditionafterthe stoppageof work caused by such tradedisputehas
ceased .
(6) He must not have losthisemployment through misconduct
or have voluntarilylefthis employment without just cause but this
conditionshallhave effectonly forsixweeks or such lessperiodas the
Board may determine afterthe date of his losingor leavinghis em-
ployment .
(7) He must not be an inmate ofany prisonor workhouse or other
institutionsupportedwholly or partlyout of publicfunds.
(8) He must not be residenttemporarilyor permanently outside
Northern Ireland.

## Page 132

126 UNEMPLOYMENT INSURANCE .
(9) He must not be in receiptof any sicknessor disablement
benefit or disablement allowance under the national Health Insurance
Acts (Northern Ireland) 1911 to 1922.
(10) He must not be in receiptof an old age pension under the
Old Age Pension Acts,1908 to 1919.

DETERMINATION OF CLAIMS .
7.- (1) Subject to the provisionsof the Scheme allclaims to
benefitunder the Scheme and allquestionsarisingin connectionwith
such claimsshallbe determined by the Board whose decisionshallbe
finaland conclusiveand not subjectto appealto any Court,exceptin
the caseswhere itishereby providedthat the finaladjudicationupon
the matter at issueshallrestwith the Umpire and in such casesthe
decisionofthe Umpire shallbe finaland conclusiveand not subjectto
appealto any court.
(2) The Umpire shallfinallyadjudicatein the followingcases:
(a) inany casewheretheBoardrefersthematteratissuetohim ;
(b) in any case where the Ministrybeing of opinionthat some
point of generalimportance isinvolved directsthe matter
to be so referred .
(c) in any casewhere the Board grantsleaveto appealto an
insuredperson desirousof appealingfrom a decisionof the
Board , and
(d) in any casewhere an associationof workersof which an
insuredperson isa member isdesirousof appealingfrom a
decisionof the Board affectingsuch person.
(3) The Board and the Umpire may respectivelyreferto local
refereesforexaminationand reportany matter to be decidedby them
or him under the Scheme ; such localrefereesbeing appointed in
accordancewith rulesmade by that Board .

InsuranceActs (Northern Ireland), 1920 to 1923 ;
(c) The expression" the Ministry" means the Ministryof
Labour for Northern Ireland ;
(d) The expression" the Umpire " means the Umpire for Nor-
thern Irelandappointed under the Acts ;
(e) The expression" specialorder" has the same meaning as
in the PrincipalAct ;

ployeeswhich is connected with the employment or non-
employment or the terms of employment or the conditions
of employment of any persons whether employees in the
employment of the employer with whom the disputearises

Ifforthe purposeofobtainingany benefitor payment under the
Scheme ,eitherforhimselforforany otherpersonor forthe purposeof

enablingany otherpersonto avoidany such payment, any person
knowingly makes any falsestatementor falserepresentation,he shall
be liableon summary convictionto imprisonment fora term not ex-
ceedingsix months , with or without hard labour. A Court of Sum-

Summary Jurisdictionin England inthe caseof a personconvictedfor
an offenceunder thissub-sectionof imposing a finenot exceeding

Ifany employer has failedor neglectedto pay any contributions
whichheisliableundertheSchemetopay,orifanyemployerorinsured
personorany otherpersonrefusesorneglectstocomplywithany ofthe
requirementsof the Scheme or the rulesmade thereunder,or ifany

contribution,he shall,foreachoffence,be liableon summary convic-

Where an employer has been convicted under the foregoing
provisionsof thissectionof the offenceof failingor neglectingto pay
any contributionunder the Scheme ,he shallbe liableto pay to the
insurancefund a sum equal to the amount which he has so failedor
neglectedto pay,and on such a convictionifnoticeof the intention
to do so has been servedwith the summons or warrant,evidencemay
be given of the failureor neglecton the part of the employer to pay
other contributionsin respectof the same person during the year
precedingthe date when the informationwas so laid,and on proofof
such failureor neglectthe employer shallbe liableto pay the insurance
fund a sum equal to the totalof allthe contributionswhich he isso
proved tohave failedor neglectedtopay .
Any sum paid by an employer under the foregoingprovision
shallbe treatedas a payment in satisfactionof the unpaid contribu-
tions .
Every personwho buys,sells,or offersforsale,takesor givesin
exchange,or pawns or takes in pawn ,any prescribedcertificateshall
be liableon summary convictionto a finenot exceedingtwenty pounds .

Notwithstandingany provisioninany Actprescribingtheperiod
withinwhich summary proceedingsmay be commenced,proceedings
foran offenceunder theScheme may be commenced at any time within
threemonths from the date on which evidence,sufficientinthe opinion
of the Board to justifya prosecutionfor the offence,comes to their
knowledge,or withinsixmonths afterthe commission of the offence,
whichever periodisthe longer.
For the purposesof the foregoingprovision,a certificatepur-
portingto be signedon behalfof the Board ,as to the date on which
such evidenceas aforesaidcame to theirknowledge shallbe conclusive
evidence thereof .

MADE BY THE MINISTRY OF LABOUR FOR NORTHERN IRELAND UNDER
THE UNEMPLOYMENT INSURANCE ACTS (NORTHERN IRELAND ),
1920 το 1923 .
1923. No. 56 .
WHEREAS by the Unemployment Insurance(InsuranceIn-
dustrySpecialScheme) Order, 1921,the InsuranceIndustryUnem-
ployment Scheme (hereinafterreferredto as " the Scheme ") was
approved by the Ministerof Labour forthe United Kingdom ; AND
WHEREAS by theGovernmentofIreland(AdaptationofUnemploy

## Page 141

InsuranceIndustrySpecialScheme (Grant). 135
ment InsuranceActs)Order,1922,the Scheme was continuedin force
'inNorthern Irelandasfrom the firstday ofJanuary,nineteenhundred
and twenty-two ; AND WHEREAS the Incorporated Insurance
Industry Unemployment Insurance Board (hereinafterreferredto as
theJointBoard) isthebody chargedwiththeadministrationofthe
Scheme :
AND WHEREAS by sub-section(7)of Section18 of the Unem-
ploymentInsuranceAct,1920 (hereinafterreferredtoas "theAct "),
the Ministryof Labour for Northern Ireland(hereinafterreferredto
as " the Ministry")isempowered by Regulationsmade by itwith the
consentof the MinistryofFinance to determinethe sum to be paid to
theJointBoard ineveryyear out ofmonies providedby the Parliament
of Northern Ireland,and to prescribethe conditionsupon which such
payments can be made :
NOW THEREFORE the Ministry, by virtue of the powers
hereinbeforerecitedand of allotherpowers enablingitin thatbehalf,
hereby with the consentofthe MinistryofFinancemakes thefollowing
Regulations :-
1. While the scheme isin forcethe sum to be paid under the
saidsub-section(7)of section18 of the Act out of monies providedby
the Parliament of Northern Irelandto the JointBoard shallin every
insuranceyear be whichever of the two followingamounts isin that
insuranceyear the less,that isto say :-
(a) an amount equal to one-fourthof the amount receivedby
the JointBoard by way ofcontributionsinrespectofpersons
employed in Northern Irelandproperlypaid duringthe
insuranceyearinquestionunder theprovisionsoftheScheme ;
or ,
(b) an amount equalto three-tenthsofthe amount which would,
if the Scheme had not been in force and if the rates of con-
tributions set out in the Third Schedule to the Act as
originallyenactedhad been in operation,have been paid by
way of contributionsunder the generalprovisionsof the
Act out of monies provided by the Parliament of Northern
Irelandin respectof the persons employed in Northern
Irelandto whom the Scheme applies.
2.These Regulationsmay be citedas the Unemployment
Insurance(InsuranceIndustrySpecialScheme) (Grant) Regulations
(Northern Ireland), 1923, and shallbe deemed to have come into
operationon the firstday of January, 1922.

oftheWorkmen'sCompensationAct,1906,and by theGeneralAdapta

tion of Enactments (Northern Ireland) Order, 1921, the Ministryof
Labour forNorthern Irelandhereby makes the followingOrder :-
Paragraph (2) of the Order made by the Secretaryof State on
the26thFebruary,1918,*undertheabovesection,shallbe amended
to read as follows :-
(2) A personsufferingfrom any of the diseasesdescribed
in the Schedule as dermatitisproduced by dust or liquids,
ulcerationof the skin produced by dust or liquids, and
ulceration of the mucous membrane of the nose or mouth
produced by dust,shallnot be entitledto compensation under
the provisionsof the saidsectionon account of the saiddisease
ifhe isdisabledonly for employment in the particularprocess
in which the diseasehas been contractedor other processes
involvingriskof the said disease, unlessthe judge, committee
or arbitrator is satisfied that the disease has been contracted
throughlong continuedexposureto dust or liquidsin the
industry in which he was engaged at the time of his
disablement .
This Order may be cited as the Workmen's Compensation
(Dermatitis) (Northern Ireland), Order, 1923, and shallcome into
forceon 1st March , 1923.
